She helped me carefully select a room that I liked! I was deeply moved! Thank you for her care and sincerity! In addition, the two small desserts given upon check-in were particularly delicious ğŸ˜‹ğŸ˜ğŸ˜œ Thank you very much for a new day, a new place, and a new experience... The "Jiangnan Famous Stove" opposite the hotel is also good, which can meet the needs of lunch and dinner! I stayed at the Hilton in Yancheng some time ago, and stayed at the Hilton DoubleTree today. In the future, I can apply to become a member. I will choose Hilton when I go out in the future! Food, swimming, and fitness are integrated! Good hotel, high quality, happy! Comfortable! Like myself!
The only drawback is that the upgraded 11th floor of the hotel's executive floor actually has no desk lamps, coffee cups, and ğŸ´equipment for guests to eat on their own. The answer I got after asking is indeed true. According to my experience, these should be standard in all four-star and above hotels! ? It should be improved as appropriate! Also, our flight back to Beijing yesterday was around 5pm. I applied for an extension from the green-clad waiter at the front desk early in the morning, and was told that "it's only until 2pm, you can't stay on time, otherwise you will be charged a half-day accommodation fee." I also mentioned that I am a Ctrip Diamond Card and I have four extension coupons, but I was still rejected without any empathy! I understand the hotel's regulations very well, but I hope that it will be flexible and increased to 2:30pm according to different people? As a result, my 70-year-old man sat in the lobby for more than an hour yesterday, which was very unpleasant! I deeply felt that entering the store was like a spring breeze, and snacks were given and smiles were given. When leaving the store, "It has nothing to do with me" and "You have money to stay longer." It's none of my business, a cold reception for a cone business? !
But, anyway, I still want to give a thumbs up to this hotel. During the May Day holiday, there were huge crowds of people for breakfast. The hotel staff were dedicated to their duties, especially the two older gentlemen who were managers or supervisors and were very busy. The two cleaners with short hair and ponytails on the 11th floor were also very professional and enthusiastic. I would like to thank them all here!

The service is purely because of the good service attitude of the front desk lady, otherwise I don't want to give a single point. I don't know what the entry standards for the hotel's security guards are? Is the training done in the early stage "tailored to the person". We stayed for a total of two nights. Because there were basically tourist activities the next day, we had to go out very early in the morning. The parking spaces on the underground first floor of the hotel were very tight and difficult to park. So on the first night, we returned to the hotel at more than ten o'clock and saw that there were still two empty spaces at the door ready to park. The reason why security guard 1 refused us was that these two locations were aisles (actually not) and other cars were leaving soon. It was less than eight o'clock the next morning. We set out and saw that both parking spaces were parked (a G-Class and a Porsche), and the other so-called cars that were leaving soon were still there. We came back at eleven o'clock that night and saw that there were empty spaces at the door again. We also told security guard 2 that day that we would leave before seven o'clock the next day. Security guard 2 still replied that it was not allowed. And this time when I asked why other cars could park their cars, the reply was that these cars were all the leaders' cars??? At first, the front desk said that we could park the car. After the front desk agreed, he said that we needed the approval of the leader, and jokingly said, "You can drive in if the leader agrees!" Later, after the leader came over and agreed, he kept muttering, "Leader, you agreed." I was really amazed. The security guard at the door, as the first service staff of the hotel to receive customers, had such a funny attitude. Or is it that the per capita income in Quzhou is relatively high, and our 300,000 yuan car may be embarrassing to park at the door of the hotel in his eyes? ? ?

Two-thirds of the table was filled with leftovers from the guests, one or two waiters were cleaning up, and two or three managers were standing chatting. There was very little food on the dining table, and when I saw two big steamers, I thought about eating a bun, after all, I had business in the morning. When I opened the steamer, I saw that there were no buns at all. I asked casually about the buns. There was an aunt on the waiting table. She said that you should wait for ten minutes. After that, I took a bag of frozen buns. , I lost my appetite in an instant, and decided to complain to the lobby manager, and told the manager that I couldn't eat such a breakfast, please refund my breakfast money, and I will also give an honest review on Ctrip. Immediately, I could only go upstairs to get dressed and go out for breakfast. The hotel is still in the new area, and there is very little breakfast.
